    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        数据类型映射 
            
           
          
         
        
       
      
        \boxed{\text{数据类型映射}}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.3633em; vertical-align: -0.34em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
           <span class="vlist-r">
            <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0233em;">
             <span class="" style="top: -3.3633em;">
              <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.3633em;">
              </span>
              <span class="boxpad">
               <span class="mord">
                <span class="mord">
                 <span class="mord text">
                  <span class="mord cjk_fallback">
                   数据类型映射
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="" style="top: -3.0233em;">
              <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.3633em;">
              </span>
              <span class="stretchy fbox" style="height: 1.3633em; border-style: solid; border-width: 0.04em;">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-s">
             ​
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="vlist-r">
            <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.34em;">
             <span class="">
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ：
    </p>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        SQLite类型
       </th>
       <th>
        Java类型
       </th>
       <th>
        特殊处理逻辑
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        INTEGER
       </td>
       <td>
        int/long
       </td>
       <td>
        自动处理64位整数
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        REAL
       </td>
       <td>
        double
       </td>
       <td>
        NaN特殊处理
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        TEXT
       </td>
       <td>
        String
       </td>
       <td>
        UTF-8编码强制转换
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        BLOB
       </td>
       <td>
        byte[]
       </td>
       <td>
        直接二进制传输
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        重要限制： 
         
        
       
      
        \textcolor{red}{\textbf{重要限制：}}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord text" style="color: red;">
          <span class="mord textbf cjk_fallback" style="color: red;">
           重要限制：
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      不支持
      <span class="katex--inline">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         存储过程 
          
         
        
       
         \textcolor{red}{存储过程}
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord cjk_fallback" style="color: red;">
           存储过程
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </li>
     <li>
      批量插入需手动使用事务：
      <pre><code class="prism language-java">conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setAutoCommit</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span> pstmt <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">int</span> i<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> i<span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token number">1000</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> i<span class="token operator">++</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        pstmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"data"</span><span class="token operator">+</span>i<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        pstmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">addBatch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>i <span class="token operator">%</span> <span class="token number">100</span> <span class="token operator">==</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> pstmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeBatch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">commit</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">rollback</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        性能优化建议 
         
        
       
      
        \textcolor{blue}{\textbf{性能优化建议}}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord text" style="color: blue;">
          <span class="mord textbf cjk_fallback" style="color: blue;">
           性能优化建议
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      启用
      <span class="katex--inline">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         W 
          
         
           A 
          
         
           L 
          
         
           模式 
          
         
        
       
         \textcolor{red}{WAL模式}
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em; color: red;">
           W
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="color: red;">
           A
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="color: red;">
           L
          </span>
          <span class="mord cjk_fallback" style="color: red;">
           模式
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      （Write-Ahead Logging）：
      <pre><code class="prism language-sql">PRAGMA journal_mode<span class="token operator">=</span>WAL<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     </li>
     <li>
      设置合理
      <span class="katex--inline">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         缓存大小 
          
         
        
       
         \textcolor{red}{缓存大小}
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord cjk_fallback" style="color: red;">
           缓存大小
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      ：
      <pre><code class="prism language-sql">PRAGMA cache_size<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">2000</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>  <span class="token comment">-- 2MB缓存</span>
</code></pre>
     </li>
     <li>
      使用
      <span class="katex--inline">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         预编译语句 
          
         
        
       
         \textcolor{red}{预编译语句}
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord cjk_fallback" style="color: red;">
           预编译语句
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      ：
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 优于普通Statement</span>
<span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span> pstmt <span class="token operator">=</span> conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">prepareStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>
    <span class="token string">"SELECT * FROM logs WHERE timestamp BETWEEN ? AND ?"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">

            SQ
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="color: orange;">

             E
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0576em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight" style="color: orange;">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0502em; color: orange;">
                   B
                  </span>

                </span>

               <span class="vlist-s">

              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                <span class="">

             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em; color: orange;">

       <li>
        增加超时时间：
        <pre><code class="prism language-sql">PRAGMA busy_timeout<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">30000</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>  <span class="token comment">-- 30秒</span>

          \textcolor{orange}{文件锁冲突}

         <span class="katex-html">

        \textcolor{blue}{\textbf{驱动选择建议}}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord text" style="color: blue;">

    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        使用场景
       </th>
       <th>
        推荐驱动版本
       </th>
       <th>
        原因说明
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        安卓开发
       </td>
       <td>
        3.36.0
       </td>
       <td>
        兼容旧版Android API
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        高并发写入
       </td>
       <td>
        ≥3.34.0
       </td>
       <td>
        WAL模式性能优化
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        JSON数据操作
       </td>
       <td>
        ≥3.38.0
       </td>
       <td>
        原生JSON支持
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        验证驱动是否正常工作： 
         
        
       
      
        \textcolor{green}{\textit{验证驱动是否正常工作：}}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord text" style="color: green;">
          <span class="mord textit cjk_fallback" style="color: green;">
           验证驱动是否正常工作：
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverCheck</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> conn <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">DatabaseMetaData</span> meta <span class="token operator">=</span> conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMetaData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"驱动版本："</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> meta<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getDriverVersion</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"SQLite版本："</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> 
                conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">createStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                   <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeQuery</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"select sqlite_version()"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                   <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        重要安全建议： 
         
        
       
      
        \textcolor{red}{\textbf{重要安全建议：}}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord text" style="color: red;">
          <span class="mord textbf cjk_fallback" style="color: red;">
           重要安全建议：
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      禁用危险PRAGMA：
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 在连接参数中禁用危险功能</span>
jdbc<span class="token operator">:</span>sqlite<span class="token operator">:</span><span class="token operator">/</span>path<span class="token operator">/</span><span class="token keyword">to</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>db<span class="token operator">?</span>enable_load_extension<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">false</span>
</code></pre>
     </li>
     <li>
      输入参数必须使用
      <span class="katex--inline">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         P 
          
         
           r 
          
         
           e 
          
         
           p 
          
         
           a 
          
         
           r 
          
         
           e 
          
         
           d 
          
         
           S 
          
         
           t 
          
         
           a 
          
         
           t 
          
         
           e 
          
         
           m 
          
         
           e 
          
         
           n 
          
         
           t 
          
         
        
       
         \textcolor{red}{PreparedStatement}
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em; color: red;">
           P
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="color: red;">
           re
          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="color: red;">

          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="color: red;">

          </span>
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="color: red;">

          </span>

         </span>

       </span>
      </span>
      防御SQL注入
     </li>

    </p>
    <p>
     以下是关于SQLite JDBC驱动的详细说明，结合最新检索结果整理：
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        一、SQLite JDBC驱动的作用
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     SQLite JDBC驱动是Java连接SQLite数据库的核心组件，它实现了JDBC API接口，允许Java程序通过标准SQL语句操作SQLite数据库文件。其特点包括：
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      轻量级
     </strong>
     ：驱动仅包含一个JAR文件，无需额外依赖。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      跨平台
     </strong>
     ：支持Windows、Linux、macOS等操作系统。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      事务支持
     </strong>
     ：完整支持ACID事务，保证数据一致性。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        二、驱动下载与版本选择
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        下载方式
       </strong>
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        Maven依赖
       </strong>
       （推荐）：在
       <code>
        pom.xml
       </code>
       中添加以下依赖（版本号可按需调整）：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>dependency</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>groupId</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>org.xerial<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>groupId</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>artifactId</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>sqlite-jdbc<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>artifactId</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>version</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>3.7.2<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>version</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> <span class="token comment">&lt;!-- 最新稳定版 --&gt;</span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>dependency</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        手动下载
       </strong>
       ：从
       <a href="https://github.com/xerial/sqlite-jdbc/releases">
        SQLite JDBC官网
       </a>
       或Maven仓库下载JAR包。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        版本选择建议
       </strong>
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        Xerial官方驱动
       </strong>
       （推荐）：集成多平台本地库，性能最优，但体积较大（约3MB）。
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        Zentus纯Java驱动
       </strong>
       ：无本地依赖，但性能稍弱，适合嵌入式场景。
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        SQLite Wrapper
       </strong>
       ：体积最小（约100KB），但更新频率低，兼容性有限。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        三、驱动配置与使用步骤
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        添加驱动到项目
       </strong>
       <br/>
       • 若使用IDE（如IntelliJ IDEA），将JAR文件添加到项目库路径。
       <br/>
       • Maven项目会自动下载依赖。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        建立数据库连接
       </strong>
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 数据库文件路径</span>
<span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> conn <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>url<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"连接成功！"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printStackTrace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        注意
       </strong>
       ：Java 6+通常无需显式加载驱动（
       <code>
        Class.forName("org.sqlite.JDBC")
       </code>
       ），但旧代码可能保留此步骤。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        执行SQL操作
       </strong>
       <br/>
       •
       <strong>
        创建表
       </strong>
       ：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT)"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Statement</span> stmt <span class="token operator">=</span> conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">createStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">execute</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        插入/查询数据
       </strong>
       ：使用
       <code>
        PreparedStatement
       </code>
       防止SQL注入。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        四、常见问题与注意事项
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        驱动未找到
       </strong>
       <br/>
       • 检查JAR包是否在类路径中，或Maven依赖是否生效。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        数据库文件路径错误
       </strong>
       <br/>
       • 使用绝对路径或确保相对路径相对于项目根目录。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        并发访问限制
       </strong>
       <br/>
       • SQLite默认不支持高并发写入，适合单线程或轻量级应用。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        驱动版本兼容性
       </strong>
       <br/>
       • 不同版本驱动可能对SQLite数据库文件格式支持不同，升级前建议备份数据。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        五、扩展应用场景
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      嵌入式系统
     </strong>
     ：如智能家居设备、物联网传感器。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      移动应用开发
     </strong>
     ：Android/iOS本地数据存储。
     <br/>
     •
     <strong>
      单元测试
     </strong>
     ：快速搭建轻量级测试数据库。
    </p>
    <p>
     通过以上步骤，您可以高效地在Java项目中集成SQLite JDBC驱动。如需进一步优化性能，可结合事务处理或使用
     <code>
      PreparedStatement
     </code>
     批量操作。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <h2>
     <a id="Sqlitejdbcurl_1823">
     </a>
     更多示例讲解Sqlite的jdbc的url
    </h2>
    <p>
     以下是关于 SQLite JDBC 连接 URL 的详细示例和场景说明，涵盖文件路径、内存数据库、URI 参数配置等关键用法：
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        1. 基础文件路径
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：当前目录下的数据库
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:test.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 默认路径</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       效果
      </strong>
      ：在项目根目录（或 JVM 启动目录）创建
      <code>
       test.db
      </code>
      文件。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 2：绝对路径（Windows）
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:/data/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 正斜杠</span>
<span class="token comment">// 或</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:\\data\\mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 转义反斜杠</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 3：绝对路径（Linux/macOS）
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:/home/user/databases/app.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        2. 内存数据库
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：私有内存数据库（默认）
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       特点
      </strong>
      ：每个连接创建独立的内存数据库，连接关闭后数据丢失。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 2：共享内存数据库（多连接共享）
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:shared_mem?mode=memory&amp;cache=shared"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       用途
      </strong>
      ：允许多个
      <code>
       Connection
      </code>
      共享同一内存数据库。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        3. URI 参数配置
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：只读模式
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:test.db?mode=ro"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 只读访问</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       适用场景
      </strong>
      ：防止误修改数据库文件。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 2：共享缓存模式
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:test.db?cache=shared"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       用途
      </strong>
      ：多线程或多连接共享同一数据库缓存。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 3：自定义超时时间
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:test.db?busy_timeout=5000"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 5秒超时</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       作用
      </strong>
      ：设置数据库忙时的等待时间（毫秒）。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        4. 临时数据库
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：程序退出后自动删除
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:tempdb?mode=memory&amp;cache=private"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       特点
      </strong>
      ：内存中的临时数据库，连接关闭后数据消失。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        5. 跨平台路径处理
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例：动态构建路径（兼容 Windows/Linux）
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>io<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">File</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">DynamicPathDemo</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> userHome <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"user.home"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> dbDir <span class="token operator">=</span> userHome <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>separator <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"myapp"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> dbPath <span class="token operator">=</span> dbDir <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>separator <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"data.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        
        <span class="token comment">// 确保目录存在</span>
        <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dbDir<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">mkdirs</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        
        <span class="token comment">// 统一转为正斜杠</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> dbPath<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">replace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"\\"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"/"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"Database URL: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> url<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       输出示例
      </strong>
      （Windows）：
      <pre><code>Database URL: jdbc:sqlite:C:/Users/username/myapp/data.db
</code></pre>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        6. 特殊场景配置
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：加密数据库（需第三方驱动）
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 使用 SQLite3MultipleCiphers 扩展</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:encrypted.db?cipher=chacha20&amp;key=mySecret123"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       依赖
      </strong>
      ：需添加
      <code>
       sqlite-jdbc-crypt
      </code>
      等第三方库。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 2：只读内存数据库
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:memdb?mode=memory&amp;cache=shared&amp;immutable=1"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       特点
      </strong>
      ：内存数据库不可修改。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        7. 网络路径（需扩展支持）
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     SQLite 默认不支持远程连接，但可通过
     <code>
      sqlite-jdbc-remote
     </code>
     等扩展实现：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:http://example.com/remote.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       注意
      </strong>
      ：需引入特定依赖并配置网络协议支持。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        8. 高级 URI 参数
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：设置同步模式
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:test.db?synchronous=OFF"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       参数说明
      </strong>
      ：
      <ul>
       <li>
        <code>
         synchronous=OFF
        </code>
        ：禁用同步写入（提升性能，但有数据丢失风险）。
       </li>
       <li>
        <code>
         synchronous=FULL
        </code>
        ：完全同步（默认，最安全）。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 2：设置页面大小
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:test.db?page_size=4096"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       用途
      </strong>
      ：自定义数据库页大小（需在创建数据库前设置）。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        9. 自动清理临时文件
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:tempdb.db?delete_on_close=true"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       效果
      </strong>
      ：连接关闭后自动删除数据库文件。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        10. 组合参数示例
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:mydb.db?mode=rw&amp;cache=shared&amp;journal_mode=WAL"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       参数分解
      </strong>
      ：
      <ul>
       <li>
        <code>
         mode=rw
        </code>
        ：读写模式（默认）。
       </li>
       <li>
        <code>
         cache=shared
        </code>
        ：共享缓存。
       </li>
       <li>
        <code>
         journal_mode=WAL
        </code>
        ：启用预写式日志（Write-Ahead Logging）。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        常见问题与解决
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        路径不存在导致连接失败
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         错误
        </strong>
        ：
        <code>
         java.sql.SQLException: path to 'test.db': '/nonexistent_dir' does not exist
        </code>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         解决
        </strong>
        ：先手动创建目录或使用代码自动创建：
        <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"/nonexistent_dir"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">mkdirs</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        URI 参数格式错误
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         错误
        </strong>
        ：
        <code>
         java.sql.SQLException: invalid parameter: mode=invalid
        </code>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         解决
        </strong>
        ：检查参数拼写和值（如
        <code>
         mode=ro
        </code>
        而非
        <code>
         mode=readonly
        </code>
        ）。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        跨平台斜杠问题
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         建议
        </strong>
        ：统一使用正斜杠
        <code>
         /
        </code>
        或
        <code>
         File.separator
        </code>
        动态处理。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        总结
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        <strong>
         场景
        </strong>
       </th>
       <th>
        <strong>
         URL 示例
        </strong>
       </th>
       <th>
        <strong>
         关键参数
        </strong>
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        本地文件数据库
       </td>
       <td>
        <code>
         jdbc:sqlite:/data/app.db
        </code>
       </td>
       <td>
        无
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        内存数据库
       </td>
       <td>
        <code>
         jdbc:sqlite::memory:
        </code>
       </td>
       <td>
        <code>
         :memory:
        </code>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        共享内存数据库
       </td>
       <td>
        <code>
         jdbc:sqlite:file:memdb?mode=memory&amp;cache=shared
        </code>
       </td>
       <td>
        <code>
         cache=shared
        </code>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        只读访问
       </td>
       <td>
        <code>
         jdbc:sqlite:file:app.db?mode=ro
        </code>
       </td>
       <td>
        <code>
         mode=ro
        </code>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        加密数据库
       </td>
       <td>
        <code>
         jdbc:sqlite:file:encrypted.db?cipher=aes-256-cbc&amp;key=secret
        </code>
       </td>
       <td>
        第三方扩展参数
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        高性能模式（WAL）
       </td>
       <td>
        <code>
         jdbc:sqlite:file:app.db?journal_mode=WAL
        </code>
       </td>
       <td>
        <code>
         journal_mode=WAL
        </code>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p>
     通过灵活组合 URL 参数，可以满足开发、测试和生产环境中对 SQLite 数据库的多样化需求。如有具体问题，欢迎进一步探讨！
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     当然，以下是一些关于SQLite JDBC URL的示例及讲解，帮助您更好地理解和使用SQLite JDBC驱动：
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       SQLite JDBC URL的基本格式
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     SQLite JDBC URL的基本格式如下：
    </p>
    <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:&lt;database_file_path&gt;
</code></pre>
    <p>
     其中，
     <code>
      &lt;database_file_path&gt;
     </code>
     是指向SQLite数据库文件的路径，可以是相对路径或绝对路径。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       示例讲解
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        连接到本地文件系统中的SQLite数据库
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         URL示例
        </strong>
        ：
        <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:sample.db
</code></pre>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         解释
        </strong>
        ：
        <ul>
         <li>
          这个URL表示连接到当前目录下名为
          <code>
           sample.db
          </code>
          的SQLite数据库文件。
         </li>
         <li>
          如果该文件不存在，SQLite会自动创建一个新的数据库文件。
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        连接到指定路径下的SQLite数据库
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         URL示例
        </strong>
        ：
        <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:C:/work/product.db
</code></pre>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         解释
        </strong>
        ：
        <ul>
         <li>
          这个URL表示连接到Windows系统C盘
          <code>
           work
          </code>
          目录下的
          <code>
           product.db
          </code>
          数据库文件。
         </li>
         <li>
          路径使用反斜杠
          <code>
           \
          </code>
          分隔，但在URL中通常使用正斜杠
          <code>
           /
          </code>
          。
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        连接到网络上的SQLite数据库（通过共享目录）
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         URL示例
        </strong>
        ：
        <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite://\\COMPUTERNAME\shareA\dirB\dbfile.db
</code></pre>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         解释
        </strong>
        ：
        <ul>
         <li>
          这个URL表示连接到网络上的共享目录中的SQLite数据库文件。
         </li>
         <li>
          <code>
           \\COMPUTERNAME\shareA\dirB\dbfile.db
          </code>
          是网络路径，其中
          <code>
           COMPUTERNAME
          </code>
          是计算机名，
          <code>
           shareA
          </code>
          是共享目录名，
          <code>
           dirB
          </code>
          是共享目录下的一个子目录，
          <code>
           dbfile.db
          </code>
          是数据库文件名。
         </li>
         <li>
          注意，网络路径中的反斜杠
          <code>
           \
          </code>
          需要使用双反斜杠
          <code>
           \\
          </code>
          进行转义。
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        连接到内存中的SQLite数据库
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         URL示例
        </strong>
        ：
        <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite::memory:
</code></pre>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         解释
        </strong>
        ：
        <ul>
         <li>
          这个URL表示连接到一个内存中的SQLite数据库。
         </li>
         <li>
          内存数据库在数据库连接关闭后会自动消失，因此它通常用于临时数据存储或测试场景。
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       注意事项
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        路径格式
       </strong>
       ：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        在URL中，路径通常使用正斜杠
        <code>
         /
        </code>
        作为分隔符，即使在Windows系统中也是如此。
       </li>
       <li>
        如果路径中包含特殊字符（如空格），可能需要进行URL编码。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        数据库文件权限
       </strong>
       ：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        确保Java应用程序有权限访问指定的SQLite数据库文件。
       </li>
       <li>
        如果文件位于网络共享目录上，还需要确保网络访问权限和共享目录的权限设置正确。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        驱动加载
       </strong>
       ：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        在使用SQLite JDBC驱动之前，需要确保驱动已经被正确加载到Java应用程序中。
       </li>
       <li>
        这可以通过在代码中调用
        <code>
         Class.forName("org.sqlite.JDBC")
        </code>
        来实现，或者将驱动JAR包添加到项目的类路径中，让Java自动加载。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       示例代码
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     以下是一个简单的Java示例代码，展示如何使用SQLite JDBC URL连接到本地文件系统中的SQLite数据库：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Statement</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLiteJDBCExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:sample.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> conn <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>url<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
             <span class="token class-name">Statement</span> stmt <span class="token operator">=</span> conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">createStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

            <span class="token comment">// 创建一个示例表</span>
            stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">execute</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, name TEXT NOT NULL)"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

            <span class="token comment">// 插入一些数据</span>
            stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">execute</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"INSERT INTO users (name) VALUES ('Alice')"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">execute</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"INSERT INTO users (name) VALUES ('Bob')"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

            <span class="token comment">// 查询数据</span>
            <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"SELECT * FROM users"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">var</span> rs <span class="token operator">=</span> stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeQuery</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                <span class="token keyword">while</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>rs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">next</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                    <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"ID: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> rs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"id"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">", Name: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> rs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"name"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
            <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>err<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"An error occurred: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     这个示例代码展示了如何连接到名为
     <code>
      sample.db
     </code>
     的SQLite数据库文件，创建一个表，插入一些数据，并查询这些数据。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     SQLite JDBC URL用于指定数据库的位置和类型。根据SQLite数据库是位于文件系统中还是内存中的不同，URL的格式也会有所不同。以下是一些关于如何构建和使用SQLite JDBC URL的示例讲解。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       文件系统数据库的连接
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     当SQLite数据库存储在文件系统上时，JDBC URL应包含指向该数据库文件的路径。路径可以是绝对路径也可以是相对路径。下面是一些具体的例子：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        相对路径
       </strong>
       ：如果数据库文件与Java程序在同一目录下，可以使用相对路径来指定数据库位置。
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:test.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       这里的
       <code>
        test.db
       </code>
       是相对于当前工作目录的SQLite数据库文件名。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        绝对路径
       </strong>
       ：如果你知道数据库文件的确切位置，可以使用绝对路径。
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:/path/to/test.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// Unix/Linux/Mac OS X</span>
<span class="token comment">// 或者</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:/path/to/test.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// Windows</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       注意，在Windows系统中使用反斜杠
       <code>
        \
       </code>
       作为路径分隔符时，需要进行转义（即使用双反斜杠
       <code>
        \\
       </code>
       ）或者直接使用正斜杠
       <code>
        /
       </code>
       ，因为后者也被Java字符串接受。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        共享文件夹中的数据库
       </strong>
       ：如果数据库文件位于网络上的共享文件夹中，可以通过映射驱动器或使用UNC路径来访问它。
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite://server/share/path/to/test.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// UNC路径</span>
</code></pre>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       内存数据库的连接
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     SQLite还支持创建仅存在于内存中的数据库，这对于测试非常有用。要连接到一个内存数据库，你可以使用特殊的
     <code>
      :memory:
     </code>
     标识符作为数据库名称。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     每次使用这个URL时都会创建一个新的、空的数据库。如果你想在同一个会话中保持数据，必须确保在整个生命周期内只打开一次这样的连接。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       其他选项
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     有时你可能想要对SQLite的行为进行微调，这可以通过在JDBC URL后面附加参数来实现。例如，设置页面大小、同步模式等。这些参数以键值对的形式追加到URL末尾，并用问号(
     <code>
      ?
     </code>
     )分隔。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:test.db?cache=shared&amp;mode=ro"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     这里设置了缓存模式为共享，并且打开了只读模式。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       示例代码
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     结合上述内容，这里有一个完整的示例，展示了如何使用不同的URL格式来连接SQLite数据库：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLiteJDBCExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">Class</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">forName</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"org.sqlite.JDBC"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 加载SQLite JDBC驱动</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 使用相对路径</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connRelative <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:test.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到相对路径下的数据库！"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            connRelative<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

            <span class="token comment">// 使用绝对路径</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connAbsolute <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:/full/path/to/test.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到绝对路径下的数据库！"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            connAbsolute<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

            <span class="token comment">// 使用内存数据库</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connMemory <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到内存数据库！"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            connMemory<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 带有额外参数的连接</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connParams <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:test.db?cache=shared&amp;mode=ro"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接带有参数的数据库！"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            connParams<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Exception</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printStackTrace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     通过这种方式，你可以灵活地根据项目需求配置SQLite数据库的连接方式。请记得在实际应用中正确处理异常，并且在完成操作后关闭数据库连接以释放资源。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     在Java中使用JDBC连接SQLite数据库时，JDBC URL的格式决定了如何连接到特定的SQLite数据库文件或内存数据库。以下为你详细介绍不同场景下SQLite JDBC URL的使用示例：
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       连接到本地文件数据库
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     这是最常见的场景，你可以使用以下格式的JDBC URL连接到本地的SQLite数据库文件：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">LocalFileConnectionExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token comment">// 数据库文件路径</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> dbFilePath <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"path/to/your/database.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token comment">// 构建JDBC URL</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> jdbcUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> dbFilePath<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>jdbcUrl<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到本地文件数据库: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> dbFilePath<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>err<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"连接数据库时出错: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     在上述代码里，
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite:
     </code>
     是固定的前缀，后面跟上本地SQLite数据库文件的路径。如果数据库文件不存在，SQLite会自动创建一个新的数据库文件。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       连接到内存数据库
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     当你需要进行临时的数据处理，不想创建实际的数据库文件时，可以使用内存数据库。内存数据库在程序结束后数据会丢失。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">InMemoryConnectionExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token comment">// 内存数据库的JDBC URL</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> jdbcUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>jdbcUrl<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到内存数据库"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>err<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"连接数据库时出错: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     这里的
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite::memory:
     </code>
     表示连接到一个内存数据库。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       连接到共享内存数据库
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     在多线程或多进程环境中，你可能需要多个连接共享同一个内存数据库。可以通过在URL中指定参数来实现。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SharedMemoryConnectionExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token comment">// 共享内存数据库的JDBC URL</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> jdbcUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:?cache=shared"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>jdbcUrl<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到共享内存数据库"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>err<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"连接数据库时出错: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite::memory:?cache=shared
     </code>
     中的
     <code>
      cache=shared
     </code>
     参数表示该内存数据库可以被多个连接共享。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       注意事项
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       文件路径
      </strong>
      ：在使用本地文件数据库时，要确保提供的文件路径是正确的，并且程序有访问该文件的权限。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       内存数据库
      </strong>
      ：内存数据库的数据仅在程序运行期间存在，程序结束后数据会丢失。如果需要持久化数据，建议使用本地文件数据库。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       共享内存数据库
      </strong>
      ：共享内存数据库在多线程或多进程环境中使用时，要注意并发访问的问题，避免数据冲突。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
