    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     以下是SQLite的JDBC URL的各种示例及讲解：
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       1. 基本格式
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     SQLite的JDBC URL的基本格式为：
    </p>
    <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:database_file_path
</code></pre>
    <p>
     其中，
     <code>
      database_file_path
     </code>
     是SQLite数据库文件的路径，可以是相对路径或绝对路径。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       2. 文件数据库的相对路径示例
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     假设数据库文件名为
     <code>
      mydatabase.db
     </code>
     ，位于项目的根目录下，则JDBC URL可以写为：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     如果数据库文件位于项目的
     <code>
      data
     </code>
     文件夹下，则可以写为：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:data/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 相对路径</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     相对路径的使用使得项目更具可移植性。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       3. 文件数据库的绝对路径示例
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     如果需要指定绝对路径，例如数据库文件位于
     <code>
      C:/work/
     </code>
     目录下，文件名为
     <code>
      product.db
     </code>
     ，则JDBC URL为：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:/work/product.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       4. 内存数据库示例
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     SQLite还支持在内存中创建数据库，这对于需要临时存储数据的场景非常有用。内存数据库的JDBC URL可以写为：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     或者更简洁地写为：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     内存数据库在程序结束时会自动销毁，数据不会被持久化。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       5. 示例代码
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     以下是一个完整的示例，展示如何使用SQLite JDBC URL连接到SQLite数据库并进行基本操作：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">ResultSet</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Statement</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLiteJDBCExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">final</span> <span class="token class-name">String</span> <span class="token constant">DB_URL</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token comment">// 1. 注册 JDBC 驱动（SQLite JDBC 驱动会自动注册，所以这一步可以省略）</span>
            <span class="token comment">// Class.forName("org.sqlite.JDBC");</span>

            <span class="token comment">// 2. 打开数据库连接</span>
            <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token constant">DB_URL</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到数据库！"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 3. 创建表</span>
                <span class="token function">createTable</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 4. 插入数据</span>
                <span class="token function">insertData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 5. 查询数据</span>
                <span class="token function">selectData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 6. 更新数据</span>
                <span class="token function">updateData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 7. 删除数据</span>
                <span class="token function">deleteData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 8. 再次查询数据</span>
                <span class="token function">selectData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printStackTrace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">createTable</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users ("</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                <span class="token string">"id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                <span class="token string">"name TEXT NOT NULL,"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                <span class="token string">"email TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                <span class="token string">"age INTEGER"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                <span class="token string">")"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Statement</span> statement <span class="token operator">=</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">createStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            statement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">execute</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">insertData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"INSERT INTO users (name, email, age) VALUES (?, ?, ?)"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span> preparedStatement <span class="token operator">=</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">prepareStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"Alice"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"alice@example.com"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">25</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeUpdate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"Bob"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"bob@example.com"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeUpdate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">selectData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"SELECT id, name, email, age FROM users"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span> preparedStatement <span class="token operator">=</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">prepareStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
             <span class="token class-name">ResultSet</span> resultSet <span class="token operator">=</span> preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeQuery</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

            <span class="token keyword">while</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>resultSet<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">next</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                <span class="token keyword">int</span> id <span class="token operator">=</span> resultSet<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"id"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token class-name">String</span> name <span class="token operator">=</span> resultSet<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"name"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token class-name">String</span> email <span class="token operator">=</span> resultSet<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"email"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token keyword">int</span> age <span class="token operator">=</span> resultSet<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"age"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printf</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"ID: %d, Name: %s, Email: %s, Age: %d%n"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> id<span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token punctuation">,</span> email<span class="token punctuation">,</span> age<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">updateData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"UPDATE users SET age = ? WHERE name = ?"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span> preparedStatement <span class="token operator">=</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">prepareStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">26</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"Alice"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeUpdate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">deleteData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"DELETE FROM users WHERE name = ?"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span> preparedStatement <span class="token operator">=</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">prepareStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"Bob"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeUpdate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     通过以上示例，你可以看到如何使用不同类型的SQLite JDBC URL来连接数据库，并执行创建表、插入数据、查询数据、更新数据和删除数据等基本操作。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     以下是SQLite JDBC URL的详细讲解及多种使用场景示例：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <strong>
       基础文件连接
      </strong>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 连接当前目录下的数据库文件</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url1 <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:test.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> 

<span class="token comment">// 连接绝对路径的数据库文件（Windows）</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url2 <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:/data/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token comment">// 连接含空格的路径（需URL编码）</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url3 <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:/path/with%20spaces/app.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ol start="2">
     <li>
      <strong>
       内存数据库
      </strong>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 创建临时内存数据库（连接关闭后数据消失）</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> memUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ol start="3">
     <li>
      <strong>
       附加多个数据库
      </strong>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 主数据库 + 附加两个辅助库</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> attachUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:main.db?cache=shared&amp;mode=rwc&amp;date_string_format=yyyy-MM-dd"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ol start="4">
     <li>
      <strong>
       高级参数配置
      </strong>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 带多个配置参数</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> advUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:sales.db?"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> 
                <span class="token string">"journal_mode=WAL&amp;"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>   <span class="token comment">// 使用Write-Ahead Logging模式</span>
                <span class="token string">"synchronous=OFF&amp;"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>    <span class="token comment">// 关闭同步写入</span>
                <span class="token string">"foreign_keys=ON"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>      <span class="token comment">// 启用外键约束</span>
</code></pre>
    <ol start="5">
     <li>
      <strong>
       特殊模式设置
      </strong>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 只读模式打开</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> readOnlyUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:prod.db?mode=ro"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token comment">// 共享缓存模式</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> sharedUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:shared.db?cache=shared"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ol start="6">
     <li>
      <strong>
       URI格式连接
      </strong>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 使用统一资源标识符格式</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> uriUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:/opt/dbs/application.db?vfs=unix-dotfile"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <strong>
      参数说明：
     </strong>
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <code>
       mode
      </code>
      ：设置文件访问模式
      <ul>
       <li>
        <code>
         ro
        </code>
        ：只读
       </li>
       <li>
        <code>
         rw
        </code>
        ：读写
       </li>
       <li>
        <code>
         rwc
        </code>
        ：读写+自动创建
       </li>
       <li>
        <code>
         memory
        </code>
        ：内存模式
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <code>
       cache
      </code>
      ：缓存类型
      <ul>
       <li>
        <code>
         shared
        </code>
        ：共享缓存
       </li>
       <li>
        <code>
         private
        </code>
        ：私有缓存
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <code>
       date_string_format
      </code>
      ：日期格式
     </li>
     <li>
      <code>
       vfs
      </code>
      ：指定虚拟文件系统
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      注意事项：
     </strong>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      Windows路径使用正斜杠
      <code>
       /
      </code>
      或双反斜杠
      <code>
       \\
      </code>
     </li>
     <li>
      特殊字符需进行URL编码
     </li>
     <li>
      不同驱动版本参数可能不同（推荐使用最新版sqlite-jdbc）
     </li>
     <li>
      内存数据库适用于临时数据处理，文件数据库适合持久化存储
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     完整连接字符串格式：
     <br/>
     <span class="katex--display">
      KaTeX parse error: Expected 'EOF', got '&amp;' at position 63: …[?param1=value1&amp;̲...]
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     建议通过实际测试验证不同配置的效果，并参考官方文档获取最新参数列表。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     好的，我现在需要帮用户解答关于SQLite JDBC URL的更多示例讲解。用户之前已经询问过Java连接SQLite的基本步骤和驱动信息，现在想深入了解URL的不同用法。根据提供的搜索结果，我需要整理出各种URL格式的示例，并正确引用来源。
    </p>
    <p>
     首先，查看提供的搜索结果。网页[1]、[2]、[3]、[4]、[5]、[7]都提到了SQLite的JDBC URL。其中，网页[1]详细列出了不同路径格式，比如相对路径、绝对路径、网络路径等。网页[4]特别说明了当前目录下的简写写法，以及绝对路径的拼接方法。网页[7]虽然主要讲其他数据库，但可能对理解URL结构有帮助。
    </p>
    <p>
     接下来，我需要将这些信息分类整理。常见的URL格式包括：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        基本格式
       </strong>
       ：jdbc:sqlite:数据库文件路径。这在网页[1]、[4]、[5]中都有提到，例如网页[1]中的例子
       <code>
        jdbc:sqlite:zieckey.db
       </code>
       ，网页[4]中的
       <code>
        jdbc:sqlite:demo.db
       </code>
       。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        相对路径
       </strong>
       ：当数据库文件在项目根目录下时，可以省略路径，如网页[4]中的
       <code>
        jdbc:sqlite:demo.db
       </code>
       等价于
       <code>
        jdbc:sqlite:./demo.db
       </code>
       。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        绝对路径
       </strong>
       ：使用完整路径，如网页[1]中的
       <code>
        jdbc:sqlite://dirA/dirB/dbfile
       </code>
       ，网页[4]中的拼接绝对路径方法。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        内存数据库
       </strong>
       ：不指定文件路径，直接使用
       <code>
        :memory:
       </code>
       ，这在网页[1]的代码段1中提到，但用户可能需要注意内存数据库的特点。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        网络共享路径
       </strong>
       ：如网页[1]中的
       <code>
        jdbc:sqlite://COMPUTERNAME/shareA/dirB/dbfile
       </code>
       ，适用于网络文件共享场景。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     需要确保每个示例都正确引用来源。例如，基本格式在网页[1]、[4]、[5]中都有涉及，所以引用[1,4,5]。相对路径和绝对路径主要来自网页[1]和[4]，引用[1,4]。内存数据库的例子来自网页[1]，引用[1]。网络路径同样来自网页[1]，引用[1]。
    </p>
    <p>
     另外，需要注意用户可能遇到的常见问题，比如路径错误、驱动未加载等，但用户的问题主要是关于URL的示例，所以重点放在格式上。同时，网页[4]提到SQLite不需要用户名和密码，这点可以作为补充说明，引用[4]。
    </p>
    <p>
     最后，组织答案结构，分点列出不同URL格式，并附上示例和引用。确保每个示例都有对应的网页支持，避免遗漏关键信息。
    </p>
    <p>
     以下是SQLite JDBC连接URL的详细示例及说明，结合最新检索结果整理：
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        一、基础URL格式
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        默认格式
       </strong>
       <br/>
       直接指定数据库文件路径，适用于本地文件系统：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 相对路径（当前项目根目录）</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:/absolute/path/to/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 绝对路径</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        特点
       </strong>
       ：无需指定IP和端口，直接通过文件路径连接。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        内存数据库
       </strong>
       <br/>
       不指定文件路径，创建临时内存数据库：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 内存数据库（断开连接后数据丢失）</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        适用场景
       </strong>
       ：测试或临时数据处理。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        二、路径格式扩展
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        相对路径简化
       </strong>
       <br/>
       若数据库文件在项目根目录，可省略路径前缀：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:demo.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 等价于 jdbc:sqlite:./demo.db</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        注意
       </strong>
       ：需确保运行时当前工作目录正确。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        绝对路径拼接
       </strong>
       <br/>
       通过代码动态获取绝对路径（推荐）：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> pwd <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"user.dir"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> pwd <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 拼接绝对路径</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        优势
       </strong>
       ：避免硬编码路径，增强代码可移植性。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        网络共享路径
       </strong>
       <br/>
       连接远程共享文件（需确保权限开放）：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite://COMPUTERNAME/shareA/dirB/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 网络路径</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        适用场景
       </strong>
       ：局域网内多设备共享数据库。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        三、高级配置参数
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        指定缓存模式
       </strong>
       <br/>
       通过查询参数优化性能（如同步模式）：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:mydatabase.db?mode=rwc&amp;cache=shared"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 同步读写+共享缓存</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        参数说明
       </strong>
       ：
       <br/>
       ◦
       <code>
        mode=rwc
       </code>
       ：读写同步模式（默认为自动提交）。
       <br/>
       ◦
       <code>
        cache=shared
       </code>
       ：多连接共享缓存。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        指定页缓存大小
       </strong>
       <br/>
       调整数据库页缓存容量（单位：字节）：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:mydatabase.db?cache_size=10000"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 10MB缓存</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        适用场景
       </strong>
       ：高频读写操作时提升性能。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        四、注意事项
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        驱动类名
       </strong>
       <br/>
       需显式加载驱动（旧版代码保留此步骤）：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">Class</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">forName</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"org.sqlite.JDBC"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 推荐在连接前加载</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        注意
       </strong>
       ：Java 6+通常自动加载，但显式加载可避免兼容性问题。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        无需用户名密码
       </strong>
       <br/>
       SQLite不支持传统数据库的认证机制，连接时无需
       <code>
        user
       </code>
       和
       <code>
        password
       </code>
       参数。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        路径分隔符
       </strong>
       <br/>
       • Windows系统使用反斜杠（需转义）：
       <code>
        jdbc:sqlite:C:\\path\\to\\db.db
       </code>
       <br/>
       • 推荐使用正斜杠或URI格式：
       <code>
        jdbc:sqlite:file:///C:/path/to/db.db
       </code>
       。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        五、完整示例代码
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">ResultSet</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Statement</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLiteExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token comment">// 连接本地数据库（相对路径）</span>
            <span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:mydb.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> conn <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>url<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 创建表</span>
            <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users ("</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                         <span class="token string">"id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY, "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                         <span class="token string">"name TEXT NOT NULL)"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Statement</span> stmt <span class="token operator">=</span> conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">createStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">execute</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 插入数据</span>
            sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"INSERT INTO users(name) VALUES('张三')"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeUpdate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 查询数据</span>
            <span class="token class-name">ResultSet</span> rs <span class="token operator">=</span> stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeQuery</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"SELECT * FROM users"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">while</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>rs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">next</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"ID: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> rs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"id"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> 
                                   <span class="token string">", Name: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> rs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"name"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 关闭资源</span>
            rs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Exception</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printStackTrace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     此示例综合了路径配置、CRUD操作及资源管理，适用于大多数SQLite应用场景。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <h2>
     <a id="SqlitejdbcurlSqlite_2725">
     </a>
     更多示例讲解Sqlite的jdbc的url如何表示Sqlite文件的位置
    </h2>
    <p>
     以下是关于如何设置 SQLite 数据库文件路径的详细示例和讲解，涵盖不同场景和需求：
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       1.
       <strong>
        相对路径
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     默认情况下，SQLite 会在当前工作目录（通常是项目根目录）创建或连接数据库文件。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：当前目录下的数据库
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:test.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 直接在当前目录操作 test.db</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 2：子目录中的数据库
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 在项目目录的 "data" 子目录下创建数据库</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:data/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      如果
      <code>
       data
      </code>
      目录不存在，SQLite 会自动创建它。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       2.
       <strong>
        绝对路径
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     适用于明确指定数据库文件存储位置的场景（如固定路径）。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：Windows 系统
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:/sqlite/databases/mydb.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 使用正斜杠</span>
<span class="token comment">// 或</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:\\sqlite\\databases\\mydb.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 转义反斜杠</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 2：Linux/macOS 系统
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:/home/user/databases/mydb.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 绝对路径</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       3.
       <strong>
        内存数据库（In-Memory）
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     临时数据库，仅在程序运行期间存在，适合测试或缓存。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 内存数据库</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       4.
       <strong>
        临时文件数据库
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     数据库文件在程序退出时自动删除。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:tempdb?mode=memory&amp;cache=shared"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 临时内存模式</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       5.
       <strong>
        使用 URI 参数配置路径
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     通过 URI 格式传递额外参数，实现更复杂的配置。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：只读模式
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:test.db?mode=ro"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 只读模式打开数据库</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 2：共享缓存（多连接共享内存）
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:mydb?mode=memory&amp;cache=shared"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 多线程共享内存数据库</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       6.
       <strong>
        类路径（Classpath）中的数据库
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     如果数据库文件在项目的
     <code>
      resources
     </code>
     目录（或类路径中），可以使用以下方式访问：
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：从类路径加载数据库
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 假设数据库文件位于 src/main/resources/databases/test.db</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::resource:databases/test.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       7.
       <strong>
        跨平台路径处理
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     为了保证路径兼容性，建议使用
     <code>
      File.separator
     </code>
     或统一使用正斜杠
     <code>
      /
     </code>
     。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例：动态构建跨平台路径
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>io<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">File</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLitePathExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> baseDir <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"user.home"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 获取用户目录（跨平台）</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> dbName <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"app_data.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        
        <span class="token comment">// 构建路径：例如在用户目录下的 app_data 文件夹中</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> path <span class="token operator">=</span> baseDir <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>separator <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"app_data"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>separator <span class="token operator">+</span> dbName<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> path<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">replace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"\\"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"/"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 统一转为正斜杠</span>
        
        <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"Database URL: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> url<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     输出结果（Windows）：
    </p>
    <pre><code>Database URL: jdbc:sqlite:C:/Users/username/app_data/app_data.db
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       8.
       <strong>
        特殊场景示例
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 1：加密数据库（需第三方驱动）
     </font>
     <br/>
     某些场景需要数据库加密（如使用
     <a href="https://github.com/utelle/SQLite3MultipleCiphers">
      SQLite Encryption Extension
     </a>
     ）：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:file:encrypted.db?cipher=chacha20&amp;key=mySecretKey"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例 2：远程数据库（需网络协议支持）
     </font>
     <br/>
     SQLite 默认不支持远程连接，但可以通过
     <code>
      sqlite-jdbc-remote
     </code>
     等扩展实现：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:http://example.com/remote.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 需要特定驱动支持</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        注意事项
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        文件权限
       </strong>
       <br/>
       确保 Java 进程有权限读写目标路径（尤其是绝对路径）。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        路径转义
       </strong>
       <br/>
       Windows 路径中的反斜杠
       <code>
        \
       </code>
       需要转义为
       <code>
        \\
       </code>
       或使用正斜杠
       <code>
        /
       </code>
       。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        自动创建目录
       </strong>
       <br/>
       SQLite 会自动创建数据库文件，但不会自动创建父目录（需手动确保目录存在）。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        内存数据库限制
       </strong>
       <br/>
       <code>
        :memory:
       </code>
       数据库仅在当前连接有效，不同连接会创建独立的内存数据库（除非使用共享缓存）。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        完整示例：动态路径 + 自动创建目录
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>io<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">File</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">DynamicPathExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token comment">// 动态路径：在用户目录下创建数据库</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> userHome <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"user.home"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> dbDir <span class="token operator">=</span> userHome <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>separator <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"myapp_data"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> dbPath <span class="token operator">=</span> dbDir <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>separator <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"app.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        
        <span class="token comment">// 确保目录存在</span>
        <span class="token class-name">File</span> dir <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dbDir<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>dir<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">exists</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            dir<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">mkdirs</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 创建多级目录</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
        
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> dbPath<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">replace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"\\"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"/"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> conn <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>url<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"数据库已创建在："</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> dbPath<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printStackTrace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     通过这些示例，你可以灵活地控制 SQLite 数据库的存储位置，满足开发、测试和生产环境中的不同需求。如果需要进一步优化或有特定场景问题，请随时提问！
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     在Java中，使用JDBC连接到SQLite数据库时，URL用于指定SQLite数据库文件的位置。以下是一些关于如何表示SQLite文件位置的示例和讲解：
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       基本格式
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     SQLite JDBC URL的基本格式为：
    </p>
    <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:&lt;database_file_path&gt;
</code></pre>
    <p>
     其中，
     <code>
      &lt;database_file_path&gt;
     </code>
     用于指定SQLite数据库文件的路径。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       示例讲解
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        使用相对路径
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         示例
        </strong>
        ：
        <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:sample.db
</code></pre>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         解释
        </strong>
        ：
        <ul>
         <li>
          这个URL表示SQLite数据库文件
          <code>
           sample.db
          </code>
          位于当前工作目录下。
         </li>
         <li>
          如果当前工作目录是项目的根目录，那么数据库文件将创建在该目录下。
         </li>
         <li>
          如果文件不存在，SQLite会自动创建一个新的数据库文件。
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        使用绝对路径
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         Windows系统示例
        </strong>
        ：
        <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:C:/work/project/database/sample.db
</code></pre>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         Linux或macOS系统示例
        </strong>
        ：
        <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:/home/user/project/database/sample.db
</code></pre>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         解释
        </strong>
        ：
        <ul>
         <li>
          这些URL分别指定了SQLite数据库文件的绝对路径。
         </li>
         <li>
          在Windows系统中，路径使用反斜杠
          <code>
           \
          </code>
          ，但在URL中通常使用正斜杠
          <code>
           /
          </code>
          。
         </li>
         <li>
          在Linux或macOS系统中，路径使用正斜杠
          <code>
           /
          </code>
          。
         </li>
         <li>
          绝对路径确保了数据库文件的位置是明确的，不受当前工作目录的影响。
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        使用相对路径（相对于类路径）
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         示例
        </strong>
        ：
        <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:classpath:database/sample.db
</code></pre>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         解释
        </strong>
        ：
        <ul>
         <li>
          这个URL表示SQLite数据库文件
          <code>
           sample.db
          </code>
          位于类路径下的
          <code>
           database
          </code>
          目录中。
         </li>
         <li>
          这种方式通常用于将数据库文件打包到JAR文件中，或者将数据库文件放在项目的资源目录中。
         </li>
         <li>
          需要注意的是，使用这种方式时，数据库文件必须是只读的，因为类路径中的资源通常不允许写入。
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        使用内存数据库
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         示例
        </strong>
        ：
        <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite::memory:
</code></pre>
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         解释
        </strong>
        ：
        <ul>
         <li>
          这个URL表示连接到一个内存中的SQLite数据库。
         </li>
         <li>
          内存数据库在数据库连接关闭后会自动消失，适用于临时数据存储或测试场景。
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       注意事项
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        路径格式
       </strong>
       ：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        在URL中，路径格式应遵循操作系统的标准。在Windows系统中，虽然路径可以使用反斜杠
        <code>
         \
        </code>
        ，但为了兼容性，建议使用正斜杠
        <code>
         /
        </code>
        。
       </li>
       <li>
        如果路径中包含特殊字符（如空格），可能需要进行URL编码。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        文件权限
       </strong>
       ：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        确保Java应用程序有权限访问指定的SQLite数据库文件。
       </li>
       <li>
        如果文件位于受限制的位置（如系统目录或网络共享目录），可能需要额外的权限配置。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        驱动加载
       </strong>
       ：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        在使用SQLite JDBC驱动之前，需要确保驱动已经被正确加载到Java应用程序中。
       </li>
       <li>
        通常，这可以通过将SQLite JDBC驱动的JAR文件添加到项目的类路径中来实现。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       示例代码
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     以下是一个简单的Java示例代码，展示如何使用JDBC URL连接到SQLite数据库：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Statement</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLiteJDBCExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token comment">// JDBC URL，使用绝对路径指定SQLite数据库文件的位置</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:/path/to/your/database/sample.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> conn <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>url<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
             <span class="token class-name">Statement</span> stmt <span class="token operator">=</span> conn<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">createStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

            <span class="token comment">// 创建一个示例表</span>
            stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">execute</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, name TEXT NOT NULL)"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

            <span class="token comment">// 插入一些数据</span>
            stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">execute</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"INSERT INTO users (name) VALUES ('Alice')"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">execute</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"INSERT INTO users (name) VALUES ('Bob')"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

            <span class="token comment">// 查询数据</span>
            <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"SELECT * FROM users"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">var</span> rs <span class="token operator">=</span> stmt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeQuery</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                <span class="token keyword">while</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>rs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">next</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                    <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"ID: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> rs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"id"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">", Name: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> rs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"name"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
            <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>err<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"An error occurred: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     在这个示例中，
     <code>
      url
     </code>
     变量指定了SQLite数据库文件的绝对路径。您可以根据需要将其更改为相对路径、类路径中的资源路径或内存数据库URL。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     SQLite JDBC URL用于指定SQLite数据库文件的位置。根据数据库文件是位于本地文件系统还是内存中，URL格式会有所不同。以下是关于如何表示SQLite文件位置的更多示例讲解：
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       基本格式
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     SQLite JDBC URL的基本格式如下：
    </p>
    <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:[resource:]
</code></pre>
    <p>
     其中
     <code>
      [resource:]
     </code>
     部分可以是一个文件路径（对于存储在磁盘上的数据库）或者特殊标识符
     <code>
      ::memory:
     </code>
     （对于内存中的数据库）。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       文件系统数据库
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      绝对路径
     </font>
     <br/>
     如果你知道数据库文件的确切位置，你可以使用绝对路径来连接到它。注意，在Windows上，路径分隔符应为正斜杠
     <code>
      /
     </code>
     或双反斜杠
     <code>
      \\
     </code>
     。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:/path/to/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// Windows</span>
<span class="token comment">// 或者</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:/home/user/path/to/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// Unix/Linux/Mac OS X</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      相对路径
     </font>
     <br/>
     如果数据库文件与Java应用程序在同一目录下，或者相对于当前工作目录，你可以使用相对路径。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     这种情况下，
     <code>
      mydatabase.db
     </code>
     应该放在你的项目的根目录或者类路径下的某个地方。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      网络共享路径
     </font>
     <br/>
     对于网络共享文件夹中的数据库文件，可以通过UNC路径访问。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite://server/share/path/to/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       内存数据库
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     SQLite允许创建一个仅存在于内存中的临时数据库。这对于测试非常有用。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     每次使用这个URL时都会创建一个新的、空的数据库实例，并且一旦所有连接都关闭后，数据库就会消失。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       使用资源协议
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     某些情况下，你可能希望从classpath加载数据库文件。这通常涉及到将数据库文件打包进JAR文件中。这时可以使用
     <code>
      resource:
     </code>
     前缀。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:resource:com/example/resources/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     在这种情况下，驱动程序会在classpath中查找名为
     <code>
      com/example/resources/mydatabase.db
     </code>
     的资源文件。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       配置参数
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     有时候你可能需要配置一些特定的行为，比如设置缓存模式或同步级别等。这些选项可以直接附加到JDBC URL后面。
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:test.db?cache=shared&amp;mode=ro"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     在这个例子中，
     <code>
      cache=shared
     </code>
     指定了共享缓存模式，而
     <code>
      mode=ro
     </code>
     则指定了只读模式。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       示例代码
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     下面是一段完整的示例代码，演示了上述几种方式的使用方法：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLiteJDBCUrlExamples</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">Class</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">forName</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"org.sqlite.JDBC"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 加载SQLite JDBC驱动</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 绝对路径示例</span>
