            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connAbsPath <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:/example/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"Connected to absolute path database."</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            connAbsPath<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 相对路径示例</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connRelPath <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:relative/path/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"Connected to relative path database."</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            connRelPath<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 内存数据库示例</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connMemDb <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"Connected to in-memory database."</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            connMemDb<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 资源协议示例</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connResource <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:resource:com/example/db/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"Connected to database from resource."</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            connResource<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 配置参数示例</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connParams <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:test.db?cache=shared&amp;mode=ro"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"Connected with configuration parameters."</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            connParams<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">close</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Exception</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printStackTrace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     以上就是关于SQLite JDBC URL如何表示数据库文件位置的一些示例和讲解。请注意，实际应用中需要确保路径正确无误，并且在完成操作后关闭数据库连接以释放资源。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     在使用 JDBC 连接 SQLite 数据库时，JDBC URL 中表示 SQLite 文件位置的方式有多种情况，下面为你详细介绍不同场景下的示例。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       1. 相对路径
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     当 SQLite 数据库文件与 Java 程序在同一目录或其子目录时，可以使用相对路径。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例代码
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">RelativePathExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token comment">// 假设数据库文件在当前目录下名为 example.db</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> dbRelativePath <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"example.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> jdbcUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> dbRelativePath<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>jdbcUrl<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到相对路径的 SQLite 数据库"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>err<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"连接数据库时出错: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     在这个例子中，
     <code>
      example.db
     </code>
     是相对于 Java 程序运行目录的路径。如果数据库文件在子目录下，比如
     <code>
      data
     </code>
     子目录，路径可以写成
     <code>
      data/example.db
     </code>
     。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       2. 绝对路径
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     当需要明确指定数据库文件在文件系统中的完整位置时，使用绝对路径。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      Windows 系统示例
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">AbsolutePathWindowsExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token comment">// Windows 系统下的绝对路径</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> dbAbsolutePath <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"C:\\Users\\YourUsername\\Documents\\example.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> jdbcUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> dbAbsolutePath<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>jdbcUrl<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到绝对路径（Windows）的 SQLite 数据库"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>err<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"连接数据库时出错: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     在 Windows 系统中，路径分隔符是反斜杠
     <code>
      \
     </code>
     ，但在 Java 字符串中需要使用双反斜杠
     <code>
      \\
     </code>
     进行转义。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      Linux 或 macOS 系统示例
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">AbsolutePathUnixExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token comment">// Linux 或 macOS 系统下的绝对路径</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> dbAbsolutePath <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"/home/yourusername/Documents/example.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> jdbcUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> dbAbsolutePath<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>jdbcUrl<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到绝对路径（Unix/Linux/macOS）的 SQLite 数据库"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>err<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"连接数据库时出错: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     在 Linux 或 macOS 系统中，路径分隔符是正斜杠
     <code>
      /
     </code>
     。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       3. 包含特殊字符的路径
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     如果数据库文件的路径中包含特殊字符，例如空格，需要对路径进行适当的处理。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#0f0" size="4">
      示例代码
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>net<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">URLEncoder</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>nio<span class="token punctuation">.</span>charset<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">StandardCharsets</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SpecialCharactersPathExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token comment">// 包含空格的路径</span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> dbPathWithSpaces <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"My Documents/example.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token comment">// 对路径进行 URL 编码</span>
            <span class="token class-name">String</span> encodedPath <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">URLEncoder</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">encode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>dbPathWithSpaces<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">StandardCharsets</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token constant">UTF_8</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token class-name">String</span> jdbcUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> encodedPath<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

            <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>jdbcUrl<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到包含特殊字符路径的 SQLite 数据库"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>err<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"连接数据库时出错: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Exception</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>err<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"编码路径时出错: "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     当路径中包含特殊字符时，使用
     <code>
      URLEncoder
     </code>
     对路径进行编码，避免因特殊字符导致连接失败。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       总结
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     根据不同的场景，合理选择相对路径、绝对路径来表示 SQLite 文件的位置。同时，对于包含特殊字符的路径，要进行适当的编码处理，以确保 JDBC 能够正确连接到数据库。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     以下是SQLite的JDBC URL如何表示SQLite文件位置的详细讲解及示例：
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       1. 基本格式
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     SQLite的JDBC URL的基本格式为：
    </p>
    <pre><code>jdbc:sqlite:database_file_path
</code></pre>
    <p>
     其中，
     <code>
      database_file_path
     </code>
     是SQLite数据库文件的路径，可以是相对路径或绝对路径。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       2. 文件数据库的相对路径示例
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     假设数据库文件名为
     <code>
      mydatabase.db
     </code>
     ，位于项目的根目录下，则JDBC URL可以写为：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     如果数据库文件位于项目的
     <code>
      data
     </code>
     文件夹下，则可以写为：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:data/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 相对路径</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     相对路径的使用使得项目更具可移植性。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       3. 文件数据库的绝对路径示例
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     如果需要指定绝对路径，例如数据库文件位于
     <code>
      C:/work/
     </code>
     目录下，文件名为
     <code>
      product.db
     </code>
     ，则JDBC URL为：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:/work/product.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       4. 内存数据库示例
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     SQLite还支持在内存中创建数据库，这对于需要临时存储数据的场景非常有用。内存数据库的JDBC URL可以写为：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite::memory:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     或者更简洁地写为：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     内存数据库在程序结束时会自动销毁，数据不会被持久化。
    </p>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       5. 示例代码
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     以下是一个完整的示例，展示如何使用SQLite JDBC URL连接到SQLite数据库并进行基本操作：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">ResultSet</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Statement</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLiteJDBCExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <span class="token comment">// 数据库文件路径，使用相对路径</span>
    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">final</span> <span class="token class-name">String</span> <span class="token constant">DB_URL</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token comment">// 1. 注册 JDBC 驱动（SQLite JDBC 驱动会自动注册，所以这一步可以省略）</span>
            <span class="token comment">// Class.forName("org.sqlite.JDBC");</span>

            <span class="token comment">// 2. 打开数据库连接</span>
            <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token constant">DB_URL</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"成功连接到数据库！"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 3. 创建表</span>
                <span class="token function">createTable</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 4. 插入数据</span>
                <span class="token function">insertData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 5. 查询数据</span>
                <span class="token function">selectData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 6. 更新数据</span>
                <span class="token function">updateData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 7. 删除数据</span>
                <span class="token function">deleteData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

                <span class="token comment">// 8. 再次查询数据</span>
                <span class="token function">selectData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printStackTrace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">createTable</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users ("</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                <span class="token string">"id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                <span class="token string">"name TEXT NOT NULL,"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                <span class="token string">"email TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                <span class="token string">"age INTEGER"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span>
                <span class="token string">")"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Statement</span> statement <span class="token operator">=</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">createStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            statement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">execute</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">insertData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"INSERT INTO users (name, email, age) VALUES (?, ?, ?)"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span> preparedStatement <span class="token operator">=</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">prepareStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"Alice"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"alice@example.com"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">25</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeUpdate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"Bob"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"bob@example.com"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">30</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeUpdate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">selectData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"SELECT id, name, email, age FROM users"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span> preparedStatement <span class="token operator">=</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">prepareStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
             <span class="token class-name">ResultSet</span> resultSet <span class="token operator">=</span> preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeQuery</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

            <span class="token keyword">while</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>resultSet<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">next</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                <span class="token keyword">int</span> id <span class="token operator">=</span> resultSet<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"id"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token class-name">String</span> name <span class="token operator">=</span> resultSet<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"name"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token class-name">String</span> email <span class="token operator">=</span> resultSet<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"email"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token keyword">int</span> age <span class="token operator">=</span> resultSet<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"age"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printf</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"ID: %d, Name: %s, Email: %s, Age: %d%n"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> id<span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token punctuation">,</span> email<span class="token punctuation">,</span> age<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">updateData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"UPDATE users SET age = ? WHERE name = ?"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span> preparedStatement <span class="token operator">=</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">prepareStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">26</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"Alice"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeUpdate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

    <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">deleteData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">throws</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLException</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token class-name">String</span> sql <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"DELETE FROM users WHERE name = ?"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">PreparedStatement</span> preparedStatement <span class="token operator">=</span> connection<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">prepareStatement</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"Bob"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            preparedStatement<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">executeUpdate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     通过以上示例，你可以看到如何使用不同类型的SQLite JDBC URL来连接数据库，并执行创建表、插入数据、查询数据、更新数据和删除数据等基本操作。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     嗯，用户想了解SQLite的JDBC URL如何表示文件位置，需要更多示例。首先，我得回忆一下SQLite的JDBC连接格式，基础的是jdbc:sqlite:路径。但用户可能需要不同场景的例子，比如相对路径、绝对路径、内存数据库、URI格式参数等。
    </p>
    <p>
     用户可能遇到的情况包括：文件在项目根目录、子目录，或者绝对路径如Windows和Linux的不同写法。另外，内存数据库的使用也是常见需求，还有带参数的URI模式，比如设置只读模式或者缓存共享。需要注意不同操作系统路径的斜杠方向，特别是Windows中的反斜杠可能需要转义或使用正斜杠。
    </p>
    <p>
     还要考虑一些特殊情况，比如文件名中有空格或特殊字符，这时候需要用URI格式转义。可能用户在使用过程中遇到路径错误，所以需要强调路径的正确写法，避免常见的错误，比如忘记斜杠或转义字符。
    </p>
    <p>
     是否需要提到相对路径和绝对路径的区别？比如相对路径相对于应用程序启动位置，而绝对路径明确指定位置。可能用户对路径基准有疑问，需要明确说明。另外，内存数据库的示例很重要，因为这是测试常用的方式。
    </p>
    <p>
     总结下来，应该分几个部分：基本格式、相对路径、绝对路径（不同系统）、内存数据库、URI参数、特殊字符处理。每个部分给出示例，并解释注意事项，比如Windows路径的写法，转义问题，空格处理等。确保用户能根据不同的情况找到对应的URL写法，避免常见错误。
     <br/>
     以下是 SQLite 的 JDBC URL 表示文件位置的具体示例及说明，按不同场景分类：
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       一、基本格式
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     JDBC URL 标准格式：
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite:&lt;文件路径&gt;
     </code>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       二、相对路径示例
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        当前工作目录下的文件
       </strong>
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java">jdbc<span class="token operator">:</span>sqlite<span class="token operator">:</span>test<span class="token punctuation">.</span>db
</code></pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        文件位于程序运行的当前目录
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        项目子目录中的文件
       </strong>
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java">jdbc<span class="token operator">:</span>sqlite<span class="token operator">:</span>data<span class="token operator">/</span>mydatabase<span class="token punctuation">.</span>db
</code></pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        文件位于当前目录下的
        <code>
         data
        </code>
        文件夹中
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       三、绝对路径示例
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        Windows 系统
       </strong>
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java">jdbc<span class="token operator">:</span>sqlite<span class="token operator">:</span><span class="token class-name">C</span><span class="token operator">:</span><span class="token operator">/</span>sqlite<span class="token operator">/</span>dbs<span class="token operator">/</span>example<span class="token punctuation">.</span>db
</code></pre>
      <ul>
       <li>
        注意使用正斜杠
        <code>
         /
        </code>
        或双反斜杠
        <code>
         \\
        </code>
        （避免转义问题）
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        Linux/macOS 系统
       </strong>
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java">jdbc<span class="token operator">:</span>sqlite<span class="token operator">:</span><span class="token operator">/</span><span class="token keyword">var</span><span class="token operator">/</span>databases<span class="token operator">/</span>sample<span class="token punctuation">.</span>db
</code></pre>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       四、内存数据库（无需文件）
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java">jdbc<span class="token operator">:</span>sqlite<span class="token operator">::</span><span class="token function">memory</span><span class="token operator">:</span>
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      数据仅保存在内存中，程序关闭后消失
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       五、URI 格式（支持附加参数）
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        启用只读模式
       </strong>
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java">jdbc<span class="token operator">:</span>sqlite<span class="token operator">:</span>file<span class="token operator">:</span><span class="token operator">/</span>opt<span class="token operator">/</span>dbs<span class="token operator">/</span>readonly<span class="token punctuation">.</span>db<span class="token operator">?</span>mode<span class="token operator">=</span>ro
</code></pre>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        共享缓存（多连接共享内存）
       </strong>
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java">jdbc<span class="token operator">:</span>sqlite<span class="token operator">:</span>file<span class="token operator">:</span>shared<span class="token punctuation">.</span>db<span class="token operator">?</span>cache<span class="token operator">=</span>shared
</code></pre>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       六、特殊字符处理
      </b>
     </font>
     <br/>
     如果路径包含空格或特殊字符，使用 URI 编码：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java">jdbc<span class="token operator">:</span>sqlite<span class="token operator">:</span>file<span class="token operator">:</span><span class="token operator">/</span>path<span class="token operator">/</span><span class="token keyword">with</span><span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token number">20</span>space<span class="token operator">/</span>my<span class="token operator">%</span><span class="token number">23d</span>b<span class="token punctuation">.</span>db
</code></pre>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <code>
       %20
      </code>
      表示空格
     </li>
     <li>
      <code>
       %23
      </code>
      表示
      <code>
       #
      </code>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       注意事项
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        Windows 路径分隔符
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        错误写法：
        <code>
         jdbc:sqlite:C:\data\test.db
        </code>
        （反斜杠需转义）
       </li>
       <li>
        正确写法：
        <code>
         jdbc:sqlite:C:/data/test.db
        </code>
        或
        <code>
         jdbc:sqlite:C:\\data\\test.db
        </code>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        文件不存在时的行为
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        SQLite 会自动创建新数据库文件（除非路径不可写）
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     通过以上示例，可根据实际场景灵活调整文件路径的表示方式。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <p>
    </p>
    <p>
     好的，我现在需要帮用户解答关于SQLite JDBC URL如何表示文件位置的问题，并且根据提供的搜索结果来生成答案，同时正确引用来源。首先，我需要仔细阅读用户的问题和提供的搜索结果，确保理解每个网页中的相关信息。
    </p>
    <p>
     用户的问题是关于SQLite JDBC的URL如何表示SQLite文件的位置，需要更多示例。根据提供的搜索结果，我需要从各个网页中提取相关的URL格式示例和说明。
    </p>
    <p>
     首先，查看每个网页的内容片段：
    </p>
    <p>
     网页[1]和[2]都提到了连接URL的格式为
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite:/path
     </code>
     ，并给出了多个例子，比如
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite://dirA/dirB/dbfile
     </code>
     ，
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite://DRIVE:/dirA/dirB/dbfile
     </code>
     ，以及网络共享路径的例子。这些例子展示了不同路径格式的使用方法，包括相对路径、绝对路径和网络路径。网页[1]还提供了一个Java代码示例，其中使用了相对路径
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite:demo.db
     </code>
     ，而网页[2]则强调了路径中的盘符必须小写，例如
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite://e:/sqlite/test.db
     </code>
     ，否则会报错。
    </p>
    <p>
     网页[3]中的示例代码使用了相对路径
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite:sample.db
     </code>
     ，并提到如果文件在项目根目录，可以省略路径前缀。网页[4]的Java示例同样使用了
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite:mydatabase.db
     </code>
     ，并指出如果文件在当前目录下，可以直接使用文件名。网页[5]详细说明了URL的格式，指出如果数据库文件在当前项目目录下，可以直接使用文件名，等价于
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite:./demo.db
     </code>
     ，并推荐使用绝对路径拼接，如通过
     <code>
      System.getProperty("user.dir")
     </code>
     获取当前工作目录，然后拼接路径。网页[6]中的例子使用了绝对路径
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite:/c:/temp/e2.db
     </code>
     ，并提到路径中的盘符必须小写。网页[7]特别强调了路径中的盘符必须小写，例如
     <code>
      jdbc:sqlite://e:/sqlite/test.db
     </code>
     ，否则会报错，并且路径应使用Unix格式（正斜杠或转义的反斜杠）。
    </p>
    <p>
     接下来，我需要将这些信息整合成结构化的回答，分点说明不同的路径表示方法，并引用对应的网页编号。需要注意用户提到的当前时间是2025年3月14日，但大部分网页的发布时间在2024年及之前，不过网页[3]的发布时间是2025年1月25日，可能包含最新的信息，需要优先考虑。
    </p>
    <p>
     需要确保每个示例都正确引用来源，例如相对路径的例子来自网页[1]、[3]、[5]，绝对路径的例子来自网页[1]、[5]、[6]，网络路径来自网页[1]、[2]，盘符小写的注意事项来自网页[2]、[6]、[7]，路径拼接方法来自网页[5]，以及特殊字符处理来自网页[7]。
    </p>
    <p>
     最后，组织这些信息，使用清晰的标题和分点说明，确保用户能够轻松理解不同情况下的URL格式，并正确标注引用来源。
    </p>
    <p>
     以下是SQLite JDBC连接URL表示文件位置的详细示例及说明，结合最新检索结果整理：
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        一、基础路径表示方法
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        相对路径
       </strong>
       <br/>
       若数据库文件位于项目根目录或当前工作目录，可直接使用文件名：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:demo.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 相对路径（等价于 jdbc:sqlite:./demo.db）</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        特点
       </strong>
       ：无需指定绝对路径，适合本地开发环境。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        绝对路径
       </strong>
       <br/>
       通过完整路径指定数据库文件位置：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:/c:/temp/e2.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// Windows绝对路径（盘符需小写）</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:/Users/username/data.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// macOS/Linux路径</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        注意
       </strong>
       ：路径分隔符推荐使用正斜杠（
       <code>
        /
       </code>
       ）或转义反斜杠（
       <code>
        \\
       </code>
       ）。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        二、高级路径配置
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        动态拼接路径
       </strong>
       <br/>
       通过代码获取当前工作目录并拼接路径，增强可移植性：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> pwd <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"user.dir"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> pwd <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 拼接绝对路径</span>
</code></pre>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        网络共享路径
       </strong>
       <br/>
       连接局域网内共享的SQLite文件：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite://COMPUTERNAME/shareA/dirB/mydatabase.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 网络路径</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       •
       <strong>
        适用场景
       </strong>
       ：多设备协同开发或远程服务器访问。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        三、特殊场景注意事项
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        盘符大小写敏感
       </strong>
       <br/>
       Windows系统中，URL中的盘符必须为小写（如
       <code>
        e:
       </code>
       而非
       <code>
        E:
       </code>
       ），否则会报错：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 正确示例：jdbc:sqlite://e:/sqlite/test.db </span>
<span class="token comment">// 错误示例：jdbc:sqlite://E:/sqlite/test.db</span>
</code></pre>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        特殊字符处理
       </strong>
       <br/>
       若路径包含空格或特殊符号（如
       <code>
        %
       </code>
       、
       <code>
        #
       </code>
       ），需进行URL编码：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span> encodedPath <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">URLEncoder</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">encode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"C:/My Documents/db.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"UTF-8"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> encodedPath<span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 编码处理</span>
</code></pre>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        四、完整示例代码
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">Connection</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token import"><span class="token namespace">java<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sql<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span><span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SQLitePathExample</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">static</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">main</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> args<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token comment">// 相对路径示例</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> conn1 <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:sample.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 绝对路径示例（Windows）</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> conn2 <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite:C:/Users/Me/data.db"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token comment">// 网络共享路径示例</span>
            <span class="token class-name">Connection</span> conn3 <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">DriverManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getConnection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"jdbc:sqlite://192.168.1.100/share/db.sqlite"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            
            <span class="token class-name">System</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>out<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">println</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"所有连接成功！"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Exception</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printStackTrace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     此示例综合了相对路径、绝对路径和网络路径的连接方式，适用于不同部署场景。
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     <font color="#00f" size="5">
      <b>
       <strong>
        五、常见问题
       </strong>
      </b>
     </font>
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        路径不存在报错
       </strong>
       <br/>
       • 确保数据库文件存在，或代码中包含自动创建逻辑（如
       <code>
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS
       </code>
       ）。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        跨平台路径兼容性
       </strong>
       <br/>
       • Windows使用反斜杠需转义（
       <code>
        \\
       </code>
       ）或改用正斜杠（
       <code>
        /
       </code>
       ）。
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <strong>
        权限问题
       </strong>
       <br/>
       • 确保应用程序对数据库文件有读写权限，尤其是网络共享路径。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     通过以上方法，您可以灵活配置SQLite JDBC的URL以适应不同文件位置需求。如需进一步优化性能，可结合缓存参数（如
     <code>
      cache=shared
     </code>
     ）。
    </p>
    <p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <br/>
    </p>
